***перебежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a> (10628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run <i>(across)</i>, to cross <i>(at a run [running])</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> čerez dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run across the road</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> úlicu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run across the street; cross the street (running)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> na nóvoje mésto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to a new place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> dorógu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to steal a march on smb; snatch smth from under smb's nose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move, to shift</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defect <i>(to)</i>, to go over <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебежать.html>перебежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятель.html>неприя́телю</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебе́гать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebežátʹ</b> k neprijátelju; perebegatʹ na stóronu protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to desert to the enemy; turn traitor</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перебивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебивать.html>перебива́ть</a> (5003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебивать.html>перебива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt, to break
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебивать.html>перебива́й</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>perebiváj</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't interrupt!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to kill, to slaughter, to slay (all)</li>
<li>to break (in two)</li>
<li>to break (all)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посуда.html>посу́ду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>perebíl</b> vsju posúdu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He broke all the dishes.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</ul></li>


<li>n class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Здесь они были совершенно развязны, щупали без церемонии книги и картины, желая узнать доброту товара, и смело <b>перебива́ли</b> цену, набавляемую графами-знатоками. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Наличные офицеры не могли этим обижаться; те у них ничего не отнимали, ибо со дня отпуска они выходили из комплекта, следовательно, ни жалования, ни ваканций один у другого не <b>перебивал</b>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебиваться.html>перебива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебиться.html>переби́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to shatter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of all or many things</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be interrupted or disturbed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to survive with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to live off <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, a specified type of work</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебивать.html>перебива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***перебирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a> (3955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sort out, to look through</li>
<li>to finger (strings of a string musical instrument)</li>
<li>to take in excess, to take too much</li>
<li>to recall, to turn over in one's mind</li>
<li>to be picky, to be choosy</li>
<li>to move (one's feet), to advance (slowly)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebirátʹ</b> nogámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag one's feet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́р</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perebór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***перебить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a> (2164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебивать.html>перебива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to interrupt, to break
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́л</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On snóva menjá <b>perebíl</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He interrupted me again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to kill, to slaughter, to slay (all)</li>
<li>to break (in two)</li>
<li>to break (all)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посуда.html>посу́ду</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>perebíl</b> vsju posúdu.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He broke all the dishes.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебиться.html>переби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебиваться.html>перебива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to shatter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of all or many things</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be interrupted or disturbed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to survive with difficulty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to live off <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, a specified type of work</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебить.html>переби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебой.html>перебо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебой.html>перебо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебой.html>перебо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебой.html>перебо́ев</a></b>)

<ol><li>stoppage, interruption

<li>irregularity, misfire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intermission

***переболевший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переболевший.html>переболе́вший</a> (27000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переболевший.html>переболе́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebolévšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переболеть.html>переболе́ть</a> (27000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болеть.html>боле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bolétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переболеть.html>переболе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переболева́ть</b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to experience, to suffer (a disease)</li>
<li>to experience, to suffer (many diseases)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to experience (heartache, sorrow, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overcome (a crush, an infatuation)</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переболеть.html>переболе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переболева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grieve <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the soul or heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to hurt, to be painful <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of many or various body parts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***перебор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́р</a> (16238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> running over the strings, fingering, arpeggio</li>
<li>excess, surplus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́р</a></b>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto uže <b>perebór</b>!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">that's really too much!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>search, rundown, exhaustion, exhaustive search
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебор.html>перебо́р</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нтов</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebór</b> vozmóžnyx variántov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">examination of options</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> funeral bells</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***переборка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рка</a> (21630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the nominal combining stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перебор-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebor-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from the present tense stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перебер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereber-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with Indo-European <i>o</i>-vocalization characteristic of deverbal nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sorting through</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sorting out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> collecting of disassembled parts <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for the purpose of repair</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bulkhead, partition</li></ol>

***перебороть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебороть.html>переборо́ть</a> (28707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-боро́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-borótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебороть.html>переборо́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereborótʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переба́рывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overcome; to get the better of</li>
<li>to suppress (e.g. a strong feeling, addiction, etc.)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">

<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

***переборщить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переборщить.html>переборщи́ть</a> (26400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Dal, from dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">борщить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borščitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour a lot to no avail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:борщ.html>борщ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boršč</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">borscht</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>? Per Chernykh, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборка.html>перебо́рка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebórka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sorting through</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, through the intermediate sense "to be too picky".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переборщить.html>переборщи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereborščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переба́рщивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overdo it, to go too far</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переба́рщивание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perebárščivanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***перебрасывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a> (16785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw over, to throw across
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrásyvatʹ</b> čérez plečó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fling over one's shoulder; to shoulder</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мост.html>мост</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrásyvatʹ</b> most čérez réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw a bridge across a river</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to transfer, to redeploy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здуху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrásyvatʹ</b> po vózduxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to airlift</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shift <i>(onto)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занностей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrásyvatʹ</b> na kovó-libo častʹ svoíx objázannostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shift some of one's responsibilities onto someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переброска.html>перебро́ска</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perebróska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переброс</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perebros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасываться.html>перебра́сываться</a> (20462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасываться.html>перебра́сываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebrásyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перебро́ситься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush, to hurry <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">through or to somewhere</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread quickly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of a fire</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to defect <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to the enemy</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to throw at each other <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to quickly exchange <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, words, comments, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to play (a game) with someone <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a> (9260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебирать.html>перебира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sort out, to look through</li>
<li>to finger (strings of a string musical instrument)</li>
<li>to take in excess, to take too much</li>
<li>to recall, to turn over in one's mind</li>
<li>to be picky, to be choosy</li>
<li>to move (one's feet), to advance (slowly)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrátʹ</b> nogámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drag one's feet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебраться.html>перебра́ться</a> (5232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебраться.html>перебра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебираться.html>перебира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get over (an obstacle or to a place), to cross</li>
<li>to move (to some place)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрать.html>перебра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perebrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a> (6975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perebrósitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перебрасывать.html>перебра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw over, to throw across
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrósitʹ</b> čérez plečó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fling over one's shoulder; to shoulder</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мост.html>мост</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrósitʹ</b> most čérez réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw a bridge across a river</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to transfer, to redeploy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здуху</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrósitʹ</b> po vózduxu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to airlift</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shift <i>(onto)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перебросить.html>перебро́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занностей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perebrósitʹ</b> na kovó-libo častʹ svoíx objázannostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shift some of one's responsibilities onto someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
